<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun"><a href = vnd.unilang:noun.html>Noun</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:malt.html>malt</a></strong> (<i><a href = vnd.unilang:countable.html>countable</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> uncountable</i>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:plural.html>plural</a></i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:malt.html>malts</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><a href="Verb"><a href = vnd.unilang:malt.html>Malted</a></a> <a href = vnd.unilang:grain.html>grain</a> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">sprouted <a href = vnd.unilang:grain.html>grain</a></span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span> (usually <a href = vnd.unilang:barley.html>barley</a>), used <a href = vnd.unilang:in.html>in</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:brew.html>brewing</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:and.html>and</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:otherwise.html>otherwise</a>.</li>
